1: # Codex Discussion Position - StaffOrdersMobile
2: Chain: staffordersmobile-260413-175015-be0e
3: Topic: ÐŸÐ¡Ð¡Ðš: Ð ÐµÐ²ÑŒÑŽ Ñ‡ÐµÑ€Ð½Ð¾Ð²Ð¸ÐºÐ° ÐšÐ¡-Ð¿Ñ€Ð¾Ð¼Ð¿Ñ‚Ð° - SOM Batch A Android Quick-Fix
4: 
5: ## Questions Analyzed
6: 
7: ### Q1: Fix 1 - guest counter should count unique guests, not orders
8: **Recommendation:** âŒ Rewrite needed. Keep the behavioral goal, but rewrite the prompt to target the active table-card headers in `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, not the commented-out blocks. Recommend a small helper such as `countUniqueGuests(orders)` and apply it to all active section headers that show `guests Â· dishes`.
9: 
10: **Reasoning:** The desired behavior is clear and correct for waiter UX: guest count is coverage, dish count is workload. The problem is prompt targeting. The cited lines `670`, `680`, and `708` are inside a commented-out JSX block (`/* ... */` runs through line `785`), so an implementor can easily patch dead code. The same stale pattern appears again in another commented block around `1281`, `1291`, and `1319`. The active table-card headers are around `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, and `2337`. The grep hint `HALL_UI_TEXT.guests` is too broad because it returns both dead and live matches. Also, `countRows()` is only dish-row logic at `2004-2007`; it is not the source of the guest-count bug.
11: 
12: **Trade-offs:** Rewriting the prompt adds a little upfront precision work, but it prevents wasted edits in commented code and avoids duplicated inline `new Set(...)` expressions scattered across several headers.
13: 
14: **Mobile UX:** On a 375px waiter screen, the header summary is a scanning aid. Showing `2 guests` for one person with two dishes exaggerates table load and can distort triage when staff are moving quickly.
15: 
16: ### Q2: Fix 2 - table card disappears after "Ð’Ñ‹Ð´Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð²ÑÐµ (N)"
17: **Recommendation:** âŒ Rewrite needed. The prompt should target the earlier order-source filter first, then keep tab filtering/count logic consistent. It also needs an explicit source of truth for "table still open".
18: 
19: **Reasoning:** The proposed fix location is not the real root cause. The draft points to `filteredGroups`/`tabCounts` around `3792-3815`, but the table can already disappear earlier in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`. In that filter, finish-stage hall orders are excluded when `o.status === 'served'`, so once all dishes are served there may be no hall orders left to build a group from. Patching only `filteredGroups` will not restore a card that never reaches `orderGroups`. The prompt is also underspecified about the "table session still open" check: `group.tableSession?.status` does not exist in the current group model, and there is no loaded table-session status in this file. If the intended rule is "keep `served` hall orders until close action changes them to `closed`", say that explicitly. If the intended rule truly depends on session status, the prompt must specify where that status comes from.

# StaffOrdersMobile Draft Prompt Review

Date: 2026-04-14

## Scope Verified

- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` is **4015** lines, not 4524.
- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` is **4524** lines.
- `components/sessionHelpers.js` is **206** lines.

The draft's cited anchors match `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`. Any implementation prompt that names `260306-05` as the 4524-line source file is already pointing at the wrong snapshot.

## Primary Findings

### High — Source file / line map mismatch

- Anchors such as `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `1780`, `2004`, `2331-2347`, `3789-3818`, and `4098` exist in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
- The same anchors do not describe the same code in `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`, which ends at line `4015`.

### High — Fix 2 is aimed at downstream symptoms, not the first break point

- The disappearance starts earlier in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, where finish-stage hall orders are filtered out once `status === "served"`.
- `orderGroups` is then built from `visibleOrders` plus active requests only at `3709-3746`.
- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` at `3789-3818` are downstream. Patching only those memos will not restore a table card that never reaches `orderGroups`.

### High — Fix 4 targets dead code and live code at the same time

- `670-720` sits inside a block comment opened at `546` and closed at `785`.
- `1281-1320` sits inside another commented block opened at `1148` and closed at `1414`.
- The live table render already promotes in-progress sections to root level at `2333`.
- `inProgressExpanded` is still live in the non-table branch at `2346` and in the reset/default-open effect at `1815-1823`.

## Per-Fix Assessment

### Fix 1 — Guest Count

Rating: **Rewrite needed**

Why:

- The draft's likely anchors `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319` are dead/commented code in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
- The live guest-count headers are:
  - `2331` — new
  - `2333` — each in-progress section uses `section.orders.length`
  - `2335` — ready
  - `2337` — served
- The served header at `2337` is an easy live location to miss.
- `countRows()` at `2004-2007` is dish-row logic. It is not the source of the guest-count bug.

Missing edge case:

- Orders without `order.guest` are currently collapsed into a single synthetic guest in bill aggregation at `1977-2002` via `getLinkId(order.guest) || "__default"`.
- The prompt should explicitly say whether the new guest counter should:
  - follow that same `"__default"` behavior, or
  - count each missing-guest order as a separate guest.

Recommended rewrite:

- Tell the implementor to patch the live table-path headers at `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`.
- Use a dedicated helper such as `countUniqueGuests(orders)`.
- Do not touch `countRows()` except where dish counts are already intended.

### Fix 2 — `closeSession` / Keep Served Table Visible Until Manual Close

Rating: **Rewrite needed**

Why:

- `closeSession()` in `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` is a shared helper. It is also used outside StaffOrdersMobile, including `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981`.
- Changing helper semantics for one waiter-page workflow is not a safe local fix.
- The real disappearance starts in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, before `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`.
- `group` does not carry `tableSession.status`. The top-level group model at `3710-3739` only contains `type`, `id`, `displayName`, and `orders`.
- `handleCloseTableClick()` at `2121-2127` can only derive a session id from existing orders. It does not have session status.
- `servedOrders` are fetched only per expanded table card at `1772-1775`, so they cannot recreate a missing top-level card.

Important implications:

- If the product rule is "served hall orders stay visible until manual close", the prompt must say what data proves the table is still open.
- If the intended proof is `TableSession.status`, the prompt must also specify where that status is loaded.
- If the intended proof is "orders remain `served` until close", the prompt still has to update both:
  - the earlier order-source filter (`activeOrders`), and
  - the tab predicates/counts (`filteredGroups`, `tabCounts`).

Recommended rewrite:

- Do **not** tell the implementor to change shared helper semantics by default.
- Define the source of truth for "open but fully served table" first.
- Then patch `activeOrders` and keep `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts` consistent with that rule.

### Fix 3 — Ownership Star Badge `stopPropagation`

Rating: **Clear**

Why:

- The correct live target is the ownership badge overlay in the compact hall card, not the separate favorite star button.
- Relevant live lines:
  - `2249-2252` — `mine` badge (`★`)
  - `2255-2257` — `other` lock (`🔒`) already stops propagation
  - `2259-2261` — `free` badge (`☆`)
- `showOtherTableHint()` already calls `event?.stopPropagation()` at `2129-2134`.
- The favorite star button at `1641` already calls `event.stopPropagation()`. If the prompt points there, it is targeting the wrong control.

Small clarification worth adding:

- Say explicitly: patch only the passive `★` / `☆` ownership badges; do not change the lock badge behavior.

### Fix 4 — Remove the "В РАБОТЕ" Wrapper in 4 Branches

Rating: **Rewrite needed**

Why:

- "4 branches" is misleading in the current file:
  - `677-703` — dead commented table branch
  - `1288-1314` — dead commented table branch
  - `2333` — live table branch already root-level, no outer "В РАБОТЕ" wrapper
  - `2346` — live non-table branch that still legitimately uses `inProgressExpanded`
- The cleanup note is incorrect. `inProgressExpanded` is not dead:
  - live effect `1815-1823`
  - live non-table render `2346`

Recommended rewrite:

- Remove this fix from the batch for the current live table path, or narrow it to:
  - confirm the live table path at `2333` is already root-level, and
  - optionally delete stale commented duplicates if cleanup is desired.

## Summary Table

| Fix | Rating | Main reason |
|---|---|---|
| 1 | Rewrite needed | Wrong anchors hit commented code; live locations are `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`, and the served header is easy to miss |
| 2 | Rewrite needed | Shared helper is unsafe to repurpose; root cause starts in `activeOrders`, not only in tab memos |
| 3 | Clear | Correct live ownership badge lines exist; lock case is already safe |
| 4 | Rewrite needed | Two targets are dead comments, one live table path is already fixed, and `inProgressExpanded` is still live elsewhere |

## Bottom Line

The draft can be used only after it is re-anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` and rewritten for Fixes 1, 2, and 4. Fix 3 is the only one that is already scoped tightly enough, and even there the prompt should name the ownership badges explicitly so nobody patches the unrelated favorite star button.

+# StaffOrdersMobile Draft Prompt Review
+
+Date: 2026-04-14
+
+## Scope Verified
+
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` is **4015** lines, not 4524.
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` is **4524** lines.
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js` is **206** lines.
+
+The draft's cited anchors match `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`. Any implementation prompt that names `260306-05` as the 4524-line source file is already pointing at the wrong snapshot.
+
+## Primary Findings
+
+### High — Source file / line map mismatch
+
+- Anchors such as `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `1780`, `2004`, `2331-2347`, `3789-3818`, and `4098` exist in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The same anchors do not describe the same code in `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`, which ends at line `4015`.
+
+### High — Fix 2 is aimed at downstream symptoms, not the first break point
+
+- The disappearance starts earlier in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, where finish-stage hall orders are filtered out once `status === "served"`.
+- `orderGroups` is then built from `visibleOrders` plus active requests only at `3709-3746`.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` at `3789-3818` are downstream. Patching only those memos will not restore a table card that never reaches `orderGroups`.
+
+### High — Fix 4 targets dead code and live code at the same time
+
+- `670-720` sits inside a block comment opened at `546` and closed at `785`.
+- `1281-1320` sits inside another commented block opened at `1148` and closed at `1414`.
+- The live table render already promotes in-progress sections to root level at `2333`.
+- `inProgressExpanded` is still live in the non-table branch at `2346` and in the reset/default-open effect at `1815-1823`.
+
+## Per-Fix Assessment
+
+### Fix 1 — Guest Count
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- The draft's likely anchors `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319` are dead/commented code in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The live guest-count headers are:
+  - `2331` — new
+  - `2333` — each in-progress section uses `section.orders.length`
+  - `2335` — ready
+  - `2337` — served
+- The served header at `2337` is an easy live location to miss.
+- `countRows()` at `2004-2007` is dish-row logic. It is not the source of the guest-count bug.
+
+Missing edge case:
+
+- Orders without `order.guest` are currently collapsed into a single synthetic guest in bill aggregation at `1977-2002` via `getLinkId(order.guest) || "__default"`.
+- The prompt should explicitly say whether the new guest counter should:
+  - follow that same `"__default"` behavior, or
+  - count each missing-guest order as a separate guest.
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Tell the implementor to patch the live table-path headers at `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`.
+- Use a dedicated helper such as `countUniqueGuests(orders)`.
+- Do not touch `countRows()` except where dish counts are already intended.
+
+### Fix 2 — `closeSession` / Keep Served Table Visible Until Manual Close
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- `closeSession()` in `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` is a shared helper. It is also used outside StaffOrdersMobile, including `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981`.
+- Changing helper semantics for one waiter-page workflow is not a safe local fix.
+- The real disappearance starts in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, before `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`.
+- `group` does not carry `tableSession.status`. The top-level group model at `3710-3739` only contains `type`, `id`, `displayName`, and `orders`.
+- `handleCloseTableClick()` at `2121-2127` can only derive a session id from existing orders. It does not have session status.
+- `servedOrders` are fetched only per expanded table card at `1772-1775`, so they cannot recreate a missing top-level card.
+
+Important implications:
+
+- If the product rule is "served hall orders stay visible until manual close", the prompt must say what data proves the table is still open.
+- If the intended proof is `TableSession.status`, the prompt must also specify where that status is loaded.
+- If the intended proof is "orders remain `served` until close", the prompt still has to update both:
+  - the earlier order-source filter (`activeOrders`), and
+  - the tab predicates/counts (`filteredGroups`, `tabCounts`).
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Do **not** tell the implementor to change shared helper semantics by default.
+- Define the source of truth for "open but fully served table" first.
+- Then patch `activeOrders` and keep `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts` consistent with that rule.
+
+### Fix 3 — Ownership Star Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+Why:
+
+- The correct live target is the ownership badge overlay in the compact hall card, not the separate favorite star button.
+- Relevant live lines:
+  - `2249-2252` — `mine` badge (`★`)
+  - `2255-2257` — `other` lock (`🔒`) already stops propagation
+  - `2259-2261` — `free` badge (`☆`)
+- `showOtherTableHint()` already calls `event?.stopPropagation()` at `2129-2134`.
+- The favorite star button at `1641` already calls `event.stopPropagation()`. If the prompt points there, it is targeting the wrong control.
+
+Small clarification worth adding:
+
+- Say explicitly: patch only the passive `★` / `☆` ownership badges; do not change the lock badge behavior.
+
+### Fix 4 — Remove the "В РАБОТЕ" Wrapper in 4 Branches
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- "4 branches" is misleading in the current file:
+  - `677-703` — dead commented table branch
+  - `1288-1314` — dead commented table branch
+  - `2333` — live table branch already root-level, no outer "В РАБОТЕ" wrapper
+  - `2346` — live non-table branch that still legitimately uses `inProgressExpanded`
+- The cleanup note is incorrect. `inProgressExpanded` is not dead:
+  - live effect `1815-1823`
+  - live non-table render `2346`
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Remove this fix from the batch for the current live table path, or narrow it to:
+  - confirm the live table path at `2333` is already root-level, and
+  - optionally delete stale commented duplicates if cleanup is desired.
+
+## Summary Table
+
+| Fix | Rating | Main reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Rewrite needed | Wrong anchors hit commented code; live locations are `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`, and the served header is easy to miss |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Shared helper is unsafe to repurpose; root cause starts in `activeOrders`, not only in tab memos |
+| 3 | Clear | Correct live ownership badge lines exist; lock case is already safe |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Two targets are dead comments, one live table path is already fixed, and `inProgressExpanded` is still live elsewhere |
+
+## Bottom Line
+
+The draft can be used only after it is re-anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` and rewritten for Fixes 1, 2, and 4. Fix 3 is the only one that is already scoped tightly enough, and even there the prompt should name the ownership badges explicitly so nobody patches the unrelated favorite star button.

+- `components/sessionHelpers.js` is **206** lines.
+
+The draft's cited anchors match `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`. Any implementation prompt that names `260306-05` as the 4524-line source file is already pointing at the wrong snapshot.
+
+## Primary Findings
+
+### High — Source file / line map mismatch
+
+- Anchors such as `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `1780`, `2004`, `2331-2347`, `3789-3818`, and `4098` exist in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The same anchors do not describe the same code in `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`, which ends at line `4015`.
+
+### High — Fix 2 is aimed at downstream symptoms, not the first break point
+
+- The disappearance starts earlier in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, where finish-stage hall orders are filtered out once `status === "served"`.
+- `orderGroups` is then built from `visibleOrders` plus active requests only at `3709-3746`.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` at `3789-3818` are downstream. Patching only those memos will not restore a table card that never reaches `orderGroups`.
+
+### High — Fix 4 targets dead code and live code at the same time
+
+- `670-720` sits inside a block comment opened at `546` and closed at `785`.
+- `1281-1320` sits inside another commented block opened at `1148` and closed at `1414`.
+- The live table render already promotes in-progress sections to root level at `2333`.
+- `inProgressExpanded` is still live in the non-table branch at `2346` and in the reset/default-open effect at `1815-1823`.
+
+## Per-Fix Assessment
+
+### Fix 1 — Guest Count
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- The draft's likely anchors `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319` are dead/commented code in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The live guest-count headers are:
+  - `2331` — new
+  - `2333` — each in-progress section uses `section.orders.length`
+  - `2335` — ready
+  - `2337` — served
+- The served header at `2337` is an easy live location to miss.
+- `countRows()` at `2004-2007` is dish-row logic. It is not the source of the guest-count bug.
+
+Missing edge case:
+
+- Orders without `order.guest` are currently collapsed into a single synthetic guest in bill aggregation at `1977-2002` via `getLinkId(order.guest) || "__default"`.
+- The prompt should explicitly say whether the new guest counter should:
+  - follow that same `"__default"` behavior, or
+  - count each missing-guest order as a separate guest.
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Tell the implementor to patch the live table-path headers at `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`.
+- Use a dedicated helper such as `countUniqueGuests(orders)`.
+- Do not touch `countRows()` except where dish counts are already intended.
+
+### Fix 2 — `closeSession` / Keep Served Table Visible Until Manual Close
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- `closeSession()` in `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` is a shared helper. It is also used outside StaffOrdersMobile, including `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981`.
+- Changing helper semantics for one waiter-page workflow is not a safe local fix.
+- The real disappearance starts in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, before `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`.
+- `group` does not carry `tableSession.status`. The top-level group model at `3710-3739` only contains `type`, `id`, `displayName`, and `orders`.
+- `handleCloseTableClick()` at `2121-2127` can only derive a session id from existing orders. It does not have session status.
+- `servedOrders` are fetched only per expanded table card at `1772-1775`, so they cannot recreate a missing top-level card.
+
+Important implications:
+
+- If the product rule is "served hall orders stay visible until manual close", the prompt must say what data proves the table is still open.
+- If the intended proof is `TableSession.status`, the prompt must also specify where that status is loaded.
+- If the intended proof is "orders remain `served` until close", the prompt still has to update both:
+  - the earlier order-source filter (`activeOrders`), and
+  - the tab predicates/counts (`filteredGroups`, `tabCounts`).
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Do **not** tell the implementor to change shared helper semantics by default.
+- Define the source of truth for "open but fully served table" first.
+- Then patch `activeOrders` and keep `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts` consistent with that rule.
+
+### Fix 3 — Ownership Star Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+Why:
+
+- The correct live target is the ownership badge overlay in the compact hall card, not the separate favorite star button.
+- Relevant live lines:
+  - `2249-2252` — `mine` badge (`★`)
+  - `2255-2257` — `other` lock (`🔒`) already stops propagation
+  - `2259-2261` — `free` badge (`☆`)
+- `showOtherTableHint()` already calls `event?.stopPropagation()` at `2129-2134`.
+- The favorite star button at `1641` already calls `event.stopPropagation()`. If the prompt points there, it is targeting the wrong control.
+
+Small clarification worth adding:
+
+- Say explicitly: patch only the passive `★` / `☆` ownership badges; do not change the lock badge behavior.
+
+### Fix 4 — Remove the "В РАБОТЕ" Wrapper in 4 Branches
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- "4 branches" is misleading in the current file:
+  - `677-703` — dead commented table branch
+  - `1288-1314` — dead commented table branch
+  - `2333` — live table branch already root-level, no outer "В РАБОТЕ" wrapper
+  - `2346` — live non-table branch that still legitimately uses `inProgressExpanded`
+- The cleanup note is incorrect. `inProgressExpanded` is not dead:
+  - live effect `1815-1823`
+  - live non-table render `2346`
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Remove this fix from the batch for the current live table path, or narrow it to:
+  - confirm the live table path at `2333` is already root-level, and
+  - optionally delete stale commented duplicates if cleanup is desired.
+
+## Summary Table
+
+| Fix | Rating | Main reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Rewrite needed | Wrong anchors hit commented code; live locations are `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`, and the served header is easy to miss |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Shared helper is unsafe to repurpose; root cause starts in `activeOrders`, not only in tab memos |
+| 3 | Clear | Correct live ownership badge lines exist; lock case is already safe |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Two targets are dead comments, one live table path is already fixed, and `inProgressExpanded` is still live elsewhere |
+
+## Bottom Line
+
+The draft can be used only after it is re-anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` and rewritten for Fixes 1, 2, and 4. Fix 3 is the only one that is already scoped tightly enough, and even there the prompt should name the ownership badges explicitly so nobody patches the unrelated favorite star button.

+# StaffOrdersMobile Draft Prompt Review
+
+Date: 2026-04-14
+
+## Scope Verified
+
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` is **4015** lines, not 4524.
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` is **4524** lines.
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js` is **206** lines.
+
+The draft's cited anchors match `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`. Any implementation prompt that names `260306-05` as the 4524-line source file is already pointing at the wrong snapshot.
+
+## Primary Findings
+
+### High — Source file / line map mismatch
+
+- Anchors such as `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `1780`, `2004`, `2331-2347`, `3789-3818`, and `4098` exist in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The same anchors do not describe the same code in `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`, which ends at line `4015`.
+
+### High — Fix 2 is aimed at downstream symptoms, not the first break point
+
+- The disappearance starts earlier in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, where finish-stage hall orders are filtered out once `status === "served"`.
+- `orderGroups` is then built from `visibleOrders` plus active requests only at `3709-3746`.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` at `3789-3818` are downstream. Patching only those memos will not restore a table card that never reaches `orderGroups`.
+
+### High — Fix 4 targets dead code and live code at the same time
+
+- `670-720` sits inside a block comment opened at `546` and closed at `785`.
+- `1281-1320` sits inside another commented block opened at `1148` and closed at `1414`.
+- The live table render already promotes in-progress sections to root level at `2333`.
+- `inProgressExpanded` is still live in the non-table branch at `2346` and in the reset/default-open effect at `1815-1823`.
+
+## Per-Fix Assessment
+
+### Fix 1 — Guest Count
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- The draft's likely anchors `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319` are dead/commented code in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The live guest-count headers are:
+  - `2331` — new
+  - `2333` — each in-progress section uses `section.orders.length`
+  - `2335` — ready
+  - `2337` — served
+- The served header at `2337` is an easy live location to miss.
+- `countRows()` at `2004-2007` is dish-row logic. It is not the source of the guest-count bug.
+
+Missing edge case:
+
+- Orders without `order.guest` are currently collapsed into a single synthetic guest in bill aggregation at `1977-2002` via `getLinkId(order.guest) || "__default"`.
+- The prompt should explicitly say whether the new guest counter should:
+  - follow that same `"__default"` behavior, or
+  - count each missing-guest order as a separate guest.
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Tell the implementor to patch the live table-path headers at `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`.
+- Use a dedicated helper such as `countUniqueGuests(orders)`.
+- Do not touch `countRows()` except where dish counts are already intended.
+
+### Fix 2 — `closeSession` / Keep Served Table Visible Until Manual Close
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- `closeSession()` in `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` is a shared helper. It is also used outside StaffOrdersMobile, including `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981`.
+- Changing helper semantics for one waiter-page workflow is not a safe local fix.
+- The real disappearance starts in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, before `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`.
+- `group` does not carry `tableSession.status`. The top-level group model at `3710-3739` only contains `type`, `id`, `displayName`, and `orders`.
+- `handleCloseTableClick()` at `2121-2127` can only derive a session id from existing orders. It does not have session status.
+- `servedOrders` are fetched only per expanded table card at `1772-1775`, so they cannot recreate a missing top-level card.
+
+Important implications:
+
+- If the product rule is "served hall orders stay visible until manual close", the prompt must say what data proves the table is still open.
+- If the intended proof is `TableSession.status`, the prompt must also specify where that status is loaded.
+- If the intended proof is "orders remain `served` until close", the prompt still has to update both:
+  - the earlier order-source filter (`activeOrders`), and
+  - the tab predicates/counts (`filteredGroups`, `tabCounts`).
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Do **not** tell the implementor to change shared helper semantics by default.
+- Define the source of truth for "open but fully served table" first.
+- Then patch `activeOrders` and keep `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts` consistent with that rule.
+
+### Fix 3 — Ownership Star Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+Why:
+
+- The correct live target is the ownership badge overlay in the compact hall card, not the separate favorite star button.
+- Relevant live lines:
+  - `2249-2252` — `mine` badge (`★`)
+  - `2255-2257` — `other` lock (`🔒`) already stops propagation
+  - `2259-2261` — `free` badge (`☆`)
+- `showOtherTableHint()` already calls `event?.stopPropagation()` at `2129-2134`.
+- The favorite star button at `1641` already calls `event.stopPropagation()`. If the prompt points there, it is targeting the wrong control.
+
+Small clarification worth adding:
+
+- Say explicitly: patch only the passive `★` / `☆` ownership badges; do not change the lock badge behavior.
+
+### Fix 4 — Remove the "В РАБОТЕ" Wrapper in 4 Branches
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- "4 branches" is misleading in the current file:
+  - `677-703` — dead commented table branch
+  - `1288-1314` — dead commented table branch
+  - `2333` — live table branch already root-level, no outer "В РАБОТЕ" wrapper
+  - `2346` — live non-table branch that still legitimately uses `inProgressExpanded`
+- The cleanup note is incorrect. `inProgressExpanded` is not dead:
+  - live effect `1815-1823`
+  - live non-table render `2346`
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Remove this fix from the batch for the current live table path, or narrow it to:
+  - confirm the live table path at `2333` is already root-level, and
+  - optionally delete stale commented duplicates if cleanup is desired.
+
+## Summary Table
+
+| Fix | Rating | Main reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Rewrite needed | Wrong anchors hit commented code; live locations are `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`, and the served header is easy to miss |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Shared helper is unsafe to repurpose; root cause starts in `activeOrders`, not only in tab memos |
+| 3 | Clear | Correct live ownership badge lines exist; lock case is already safe |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Two targets are dead comments, one live table path is already fixed, and `inProgressExpanded` is still live elsewhere |
+
+## Bottom Line
+
+The draft can be used only after it is re-anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` and rewritten for Fixes 1, 2, and 4. Fix 3 is the only one that is already scoped tightly enough, and even there the prompt should name the ownership badges explicitly so nobody patches the unrelated favorite star button.

+# Round 1 — StaffOrdersMobile Prompt Review
+
+Main result: the prompt is anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` (4524 lines), not `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` (4015 lines).
+
+Ratings:
+
+- Fix 1 — Rewrite needed
+- Fix 2 — Rewrite needed
+- Fix 3 — Clear
+- Fix 4 — Rewrite needed
+
+Key reasons:
+
+- Fix 1 points at commented-out duplicate blocks and misses the live served header.
+- Fix 2 starts too late in the data flow and tries to lean on a shared helper without a safe local source of truth for "table still open".
+- Fix 3 matches a small live ownership-badge issue, but only for the passive `★` / `☆` badges.
+- Fix 4 mixes dead code with already-fixed live code and proposes deleting state that is still live in the non-table path.

codex
**Findings**
- The source-file reference is wrong. [260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx](</C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx>) is **4015** lines, not 4524. The **4524-line** file is [staffordersmobile.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx). The draft’s anchors map to `staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05`.
- Fix 2 is mis-scoped. The disappearance starts in [staffordersmobile.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:3527) `activeOrders`, before [filteredGroups](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:3789) and [tabCounts](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:3804). Changing shared [sessionHelpers.js](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/components/sessionHelpers.js:158) `closeSession()` is unsafe because it is also used in [partnertables](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/partnertables/260301-00%20partnertables%20RELEASE.js:1981).
- Fix 4 is stale against the live file. The old wrapper code at `670-720` and `1281-1320` is commented out, the live table path already renders root-level in-progress sections at [2333](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2333), and `inProgressExpanded` is still live at [1815](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:1815) and [2346](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2346).

**Ratings**
- Fix 1: `Rewrite needed`. The live guest-count locations are [2331](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2331), [2333](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2333), [2335](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2335), and [2337](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2337). The draft misses the served header, and [countRows](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2004) is dish-row logic, not guest counting. It also needs an explicit rule for orders with no `order.guest`.
- Fix 2: `Rewrite needed`. The prompt needs a real source of truth for “table still open”; `group` has no session-status field, and `servedOrders` are only loaded per expanded card at [1772](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:1772).
- Fix 3: `Clear`, if it refers to the ownership badges at [2249](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2249) and [2259](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2259). The lock case at [2255](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2255) already stops propagation, and the favorite star at [1641](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:1641) is a different control that is already safe.
- Fix 4: `Rewrite needed`. The “4 branches” description mixes dead commented code, an already-fixed live table branch, and a still-valid non-table branch.

+# StaffOrdersMobile Draft Prompt Review
+
+Date: 2026-04-14
+
+## Scope Verified
+
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` is **4015** lines, not 4524.
+- `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` is **4524** lines.
+- `components/sessionHelpers.js` is **206** lines.
+
+The draft's cited anchors match `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`. Any implementation prompt that names `260306-05` as the 4524-line source file is already pointing at the wrong snapshot.
+
+## Primary Findings
+
+### High — Source file / line map mismatch
+
+- Anchors such as `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319`, `1780`, `2004`, `2331-2347`, `3789-3818`, and `4098` exist in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The same anchors do not describe the same code in `260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx`, which ends at line `4015`.
+
+### High — Fix 2 is aimed at downstream symptoms, not the first break point
+
+- The disappearance starts earlier in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, where finish-stage hall orders are filtered out once `status === "served"`.
+- `orderGroups` is then built from `visibleOrders` plus active requests only at `3709-3746`.
+- `filteredGroups` and `tabCounts` at `3789-3818` are downstream. Patching only those memos will not restore a table card that never reaches `orderGroups`.
+
+### High — Fix 4 targets dead code and live code at the same time
+
+- `670-720` sits inside a block comment opened at `546` and closed at `785`.
+- `1281-1320` sits inside another commented block opened at `1148` and closed at `1414`.
+- The live table render already promotes in-progress sections to root level at `2333`.
+- `inProgressExpanded` is still live in the non-table branch at `2346` and in the reset/default-open effect at `1815-1823`.
+
+## Per-Fix Assessment
+
+### Fix 1 — Guest Count
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- The draft's likely anchors `670`, `680`, `708`, `1281`, `1291`, `1319` are dead/commented code in `staffordersmobile.jsx`.
+- The live guest-count headers are:
+  - `2331` — new
+  - `2333` — each in-progress section uses `section.orders.length`
+  - `2335` — ready
+  - `2337` — served
+- The served header at `2337` is an easy live location to miss.
+- `countRows()` at `2004-2007` is dish-row logic. It is not the source of the guest-count bug.
+
+Missing edge case:
+
+- Orders without `order.guest` are currently collapsed into a single synthetic guest in bill aggregation at `1977-2002` via `getLinkId(order.guest) || "__default"`.
+- The prompt should explicitly say whether the new guest counter should:
+  - follow that same `"__default"` behavior, or
+  - count each missing-guest order as a separate guest.
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Tell the implementor to patch the live table-path headers at `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`.
+- Use a dedicated helper such as `countUniqueGuests(orders)`.
+- Do not touch `countRows()` except where dish counts are already intended.
+
+### Fix 2 — `closeSession` / Keep Served Table Visible Until Manual Close
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- `closeSession()` in `components/sessionHelpers.js:158-163` is a shared helper. It is also used outside StaffOrdersMobile, including `pages/partnertables/260301-00 partnertables RELEASE.js:1981`.
+- Changing helper semantics for one waiter-page workflow is not a safe local fix.
+- The real disappearance starts in `activeOrders` at `3527-3545`, before `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts`.
+- `group` does not carry `tableSession.status`. The top-level group model at `3710-3739` only contains `type`, `id`, `displayName`, and `orders`.
+- `handleCloseTableClick()` at `2121-2127` can only derive a session id from existing orders. It does not have session status.
+- `servedOrders` are fetched only per expanded table card at `1772-1775`, so they cannot recreate a missing top-level card.
+
+Important implications:
+
+- If the product rule is "served hall orders stay visible until manual close", the prompt must say what data proves the table is still open.
+- If the intended proof is `TableSession.status`, the prompt must also specify where that status is loaded.
+- If the intended proof is "orders remain `served` until close", the prompt still has to update both:
+  - the earlier order-source filter (`activeOrders`), and
+  - the tab predicates/counts (`filteredGroups`, `tabCounts`).
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Do **not** tell the implementor to change shared helper semantics by default.
+- Define the source of truth for "open but fully served table" first.
+- Then patch `activeOrders` and keep `filteredGroups` / `tabCounts` consistent with that rule.
+
+### Fix 3 — Ownership Star Badge `stopPropagation`
+
+Rating: **Clear**
+
+Why:
+
+- The correct live target is the ownership badge overlay in the compact hall card, not the separate favorite star button.
+- Relevant live lines:
+  - `2249-2252` — `mine` badge (`★`)
+  - `2255-2257` — `other` lock (`🔒`) already stops propagation
+  - `2259-2261` — `free` badge (`☆`)
+- `showOtherTableHint()` already calls `event?.stopPropagation()` at `2129-2134`.
+- The favorite star button at `1641` already calls `event.stopPropagation()`. If the prompt points there, it is targeting the wrong control.
+
+Small clarification worth adding:
+
+- Say explicitly: patch only the passive `★` / `☆` ownership badges; do not change the lock badge behavior.
+
+### Fix 4 — Remove the "В РАБОТЕ" Wrapper in 4 Branches
+
+Rating: **Rewrite needed**
+
+Why:
+
+- "4 branches" is misleading in the current file:
+  - `677-703` — dead commented table branch
+  - `1288-1314` — dead commented table branch
+  - `2333` — live table branch already root-level, no outer "В РАБОТЕ" wrapper
+  - `2346` — live non-table branch that still legitimately uses `inProgressExpanded`
+- The cleanup note is incorrect. `inProgressExpanded` is not dead:
+  - live effect `1815-1823`
+  - live non-table render `2346`
+
+Recommended rewrite:
+
+- Remove this fix from the batch for the current live table path, or narrow it to:
+  - confirm the live table path at `2333` is already root-level, and
+  - optionally delete stale commented duplicates if cleanup is desired.
+
+## Summary Table
+
+| Fix | Rating | Main reason |
+|---|---|---|
+| 1 | Rewrite needed | Wrong anchors hit commented code; live locations are `2331`, `2333`, `2335`, `2337`, and the served header is easy to miss |
+| 2 | Rewrite needed | Shared helper is unsafe to repurpose; root cause starts in `activeOrders`, not only in tab memos |
+| 3 | Clear | Correct live ownership badge lines exist; lock case is already safe |
+| 4 | Rewrite needed | Two targets are dead comments, one live table path is already fixed, and `inProgressExpanded` is still live elsewhere |
+
+## Bottom Line
+
+The draft can be used only after it is re-anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` and rewritten for Fixes 1, 2, and 4. Fix 3 is the only one that is already scoped tightly enough, and even there the prompt should name the ownership badges explicitly so nobody patches the unrelated favorite star button.

+# Round 1 — StaffOrdersMobile Prompt Review
+
+Main result: the prompt is anchored to `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx` (4524 lines), not `pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx` (4015 lines).
+
+Ratings:
+
+- Fix 1 — Rewrite needed
+- Fix 2 — Rewrite needed
+- Fix 3 — Clear
+- Fix 4 — Rewrite needed
+
+Key reasons:
+
+- Fix 1 points at commented-out duplicate blocks and misses the live served header.
+- Fix 2 starts too late in the data flow and tries to lean on a shared helper without a safe local source of truth for "table still open".
+- Fix 3 matches a small live ownership-badge issue, but only for the passive `★` / `☆` badges.
+- Fix 4 mixes dead code with already-fixed live code and proposes deleting state that is still live in the non-table path.

tokens used

**Findings**
- The source-file reference is wrong. [260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx](</C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/260306-05 StaffOrdersMobile RELEASE.jsx>) is **4015** lines, not 4524. The **4524-line** file is [staffordersmobile.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx). The draft’s anchors map to `staffordersmobile.jsx`, not `260306-05`.
- Fix 2 is mis-scoped. The disappearance starts in [staffordersmobile.jsx](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:3527) `activeOrders`, before [filteredGroups](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:3789) and [tabCounts](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:3804). Changing shared [sessionHelpers.js](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/components/sessionHelpers.js:158) `closeSession()` is unsafe because it is also used in [partnertables](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/partnertables/260301-00%20partnertables%20RELEASE.js:1981).
- Fix 4 is stale against the live file. The old wrapper code at `670-720` and `1281-1320` is commented out, the live table path already renders root-level in-progress sections at [2333](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2333), and `inProgressExpanded` is still live at [1815](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:1815) and [2346](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2346).

**Ratings**
- Fix 1: `Rewrite needed`. The live guest-count locations are [2331](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2331), [2333](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2333), [2335](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2335), and [2337](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2337). The draft misses the served header, and [countRows](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2004) is dish-row logic, not guest counting. It also needs an explicit rule for orders with no `order.guest`.
- Fix 2: `Rewrite needed`. The prompt needs a real source of truth for “table still open”; `group` has no session-status field, and `servedOrders` are only loaded per expanded card at [1772](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:1772).
- Fix 3: `Clear`, if it refers to the ownership badges at [2249](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2249) and [2259](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2259). The lock case at [2255](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:2255) already stops propagation, and the favorite star at [1641](/C:/Dev/menuapp-code-review/pages/StaffOrdersMobile/staffordersmobile.jsx:1641) is a different control that is already safe.
- Fix 4: `Rewrite needed`. The “4 branches” description mixes dead commented code, an already-fixed live table branch, and a still-valid non-table branch.
